<analysis>
The AI engineer successfully progressed the application from its MVP state, primarily focusing on data expansion and UI functionality. Initially, critical dependency and component definition issues were resolved. The core effort shifted to massive data extraction from Daticos.com, employing provided credentials and addressing complex login flows. A significant architectural decision involved implementing a hybrid extraction strategy for TSE data due to environmental network limitations, combining real Daticos data with simulated TSE records. The engineer also began a complete overhaul of the frontend UI to make search and admin features fully functional, mirroring Daticos.com. Most recently, the focus has intensified on scaling data to 2 million records using new Daticos credentials (CABEZAS/Hola2022), prioritizing juridical entities and comprehensive personal data. Concurrently, the backend is performing a massive data migration, and the frontend is being updated to re-introduce advanced search capabilities.
</analysis>

<product_requirements>
The objective is to transform an existing React/FastAPI/MongoDB data platform, currently mirroring Daticos.com with basic login (admin/admin123) and sample Costa Rican data, into a comprehensive search and analysis tool. The core problem is expanding the data volume and types while enhancing search capabilities and administrative controls.

Key requirements and implemented progress:
1.  **Data Expansion (Current Focus):** Achieve 2 million records. This includes comprehensive data (mercantile, marriage, labor, credit, vehicle, property, company info, photos) from Daticos.com (using *only* Saraya/12345 initially, now CABEZAS/Hola2022 credentials), Crediserver.net, Google Maps, Ministry of Finance, National Registry, and integrating Supreme Electoral Tribunal (TSE) data by cédula. A hybrid TSE extraction is implemented due to API limitations. The user explicitly requested prioritizing juridical entities with owners/representatives, all phone numbers, email, labor, mercantile, and marriage data.
2.  **Administration Panel:** Develop a full admin panel for data visualization, management, user access, and customization.
3.  **Functionality:** Implement robust query options for all menu items (individual, massive, special queries), supporting massive and filtered searches with complete information, including photo queries, mirroring Daticos.com. The user recently requested restoring búsqueda avanzada with exact search by location, juridical entities, and phone numbers.
4.  **Operational:** Implement daily data updates, provide domain transfer guidance, and ensure 24/7 Emergent deployment.

So far, basic login, initial data extraction/integration, and a partially functional frontend UI exist. The immediate focus is populating the database with 2 million comprehensive records and re-enabling advanced search.
</product_requirements>

<key_technical_concepts>
-   **FastAPI**: Python web framework for backend APIs.
-   **React**: JavaScript library for frontend UI development.
-   **MongoDB**: NoSQL database for data storage, accessed via .
-   ****: Asynchronous HTTP client for web scraping.
-   ****: Asynchronous HTTP client for concurrent requests.
-   ****: Python library for in-process task scheduling.
-   **UUIDs**: Used for unique identifiers, ensuring JSON serialization compatibility (replacing Mongo's ObjectID).
</key_technical_concepts>

<code_architecture>
The application utilizes a full-stack architecture comprising a FastAPI backend, a React frontend, and a MongoDB database.

    -   **Summary**: Lists Python dependencies.

-   **/app/backend/server.py**:
    -   **Summary**: Main FastAPI application, handling API endpoints and server lifecycle.
    -   **Changes**: Integrated , , and , including startup/shutdown events for scheduling.
-   **/app/backend/.env**:
    -   **Summary**: Configuration for backend environment variables.
    -   **Changes**: Contains  and  (). Values are used for database connection.
-   **/app/backend/massive_data_extractor.py**:
    -   **Summary**: Script for large-scale data extraction.
    -   **Changes**: Modified to implement a hybrid extraction strategy for simulated TSE data and actual Daticos data (Saraya/12345 credentials). It orchestrates combined data and updates collection logic.
-   **/app/backend/daticos_extractor.py**:
    -   **Summary**: Module for extracting data from Daticos.com.
    -   **Changes**: Modified to fix login issues and successfully use Saraya/12345 credentials. Recently updated to use new CABEZAS/Hola2022 credentials for enhanced extraction.
-   **/app/backend/advanced_daticos_extractor.py**:
    -   **Summary**: Script for comprehensive Daticos data extraction across query types.
    -   **Changes**: Newly created to extract multiple data categories (approx. 396 records).
-   **/app/backend/daticos_data_integrator.py**:
    -   **Summary**: Processes and integrates extracted Daticos data into MongoDB.
    -   **Changes**: Newly created to populate the database with real Daticos data.
-   **/app/backend/daily_auto_updater.py**:
    -   **Summary**: Implements daily automatic data updates.
    -   **Changes**: Newly created and integrated into  for scheduled data refreshing.
-   **/app/backend/test_extractor.py**:

### faker.providers.passport

	fake.passport_dob()                                                         # 1975-03-10
	fake.passport_full()                                                        # Linda Evans F 13 Sep 2005 02 May 2021 02 May 2026 U73908567
	fake.passport_gender(seed=0)                                                # M
	fake.passport_number()                                                      # 500837391
	fake.passport_owner(gender='X')                                             # ('Debra', 'Allen')
